      </a>\n       </li>\n       <li class="nav-item hidden-md-up">\n        <a class="btn btn-success" href="#" target="_blank">\n         \xe2\x98\xb0\n        </a>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n class="col-xs-12 col-md-9">\n       <div class="jumbotron">\n        <h1>\n         vuestrap-base-components\n         <span class="label label-success">\n          0.8.10\n         </span>\n        </h1>\n        <p>\n         Web components that extend Bootstrap 4.\n        </p>\n       </div>\n       <h2>\n        Installation\n       </h2>\n       <div class="row">\n        <div class="col-xs-12 col-sm-6">\n         <h3>\n          Compiled\n         </h3>\n         <p>\n          Minified CSS and JavaScript with no  documentation or original source files.\n         </p>\n         <code>\n          bower install vuestrap-base-components --save-dev\n         </code>\n        </div>\n        <div class="col-xs-12 col-sm-6">\n         <h3>\n          Source\n         </h3>\n         <p>\n          Source Sass, JavaScript, and documentation files.\n         </p>\n         <code>\n          npm install vuestrap-base-components --save-dev\n         </code>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n       <div class="m-b-lg">\n       </div>\n       <h2>\n        Usage\n       </h2>\n       <p>\n        For compiled components, use it within your Vue instance like this:\n       </p>\n       <p>\n        <code>\n         new Vue({ components: { \'vs-alert\': vuestrapBase.alert }})\n        </code>\n       </p>\n       <div class="m-b">\n       </div>\n       <strong>\n        OR\n       </strong>\n       <div class="m-b">\n       </div>\n       <p>\n        If you chosen to work with source components, just import* desired component like so:\n       </p>\n       <p>\n        <code>\n         import { vsAlert } from \'vuestrap-base-components/src/components\'\n        </code>\n       </p>\n       <p>\n        and then load it in your Vue instance:\n       </p>\n       <p>\n        <code>\n         new Vue({ components: { vsAlert }})\n        </code>\n       </p>\n       <p>\n        *Note: You will need\n        <a href="https://github.com/babel/babel-loader">\n         Babel Loader\n        </a>\n        in your Webpack config file to support ES6 syntax.\n       </p>\n       <div class="m-b-lg">\n       </div>\n       <h2>\n        Examples\n       </h2>\n       <ul>\n        <li>\n         <a href="examples/basic.html" target="_blank">\n          Basic example of a landing page with selected components.\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li>\n         <a href="http://kzima.github.io/vuestrap-starter/" target="_blank">\n          Advanced example\n         </a>\n         with webpack config and theme implementation - (\n         <a href="https://github.com/kzima/vuestrap-starter" target="_blank">\n          source on github\n         </a>\n         )\n        </li>\n       </ul>\n       <div class="m-b-lg">\n       </div>\n       <h2>\n        Theming\n       </h2>\n       <p>\n        To be able to use your app theme with component\'s scss variables, you will need to use\n        <a href="https://github.com/kzima/vueastrap-theme-loader">\n         vuestrap-theme-loader\n        </a>\n        in your webpack config file.\n       </p>\n       <p>\n        <code>\n         npm install vuestrap-theme-loader --save-dev\n        </code>\n       </p>\n       <p>\n        See\n        <a href="https://github.com/kzima/vuestrap-starter">\n         vuestrap-starter\n        </a>\n        for a webpack config example with theme loader.\n       </p>\n      </div>\n      <!-- /col-xs-12 -->\n      <!-- sidebar -->\n      <div class="col-xs-12 col-md-3 sidebar-offcanvas class="col-xs-12 col-md-9">\n       <div class="jumbotron">\n        <h1>\n         vuestrap-base-components\n         <span class="label label-success">\n          0.8.10\n         </span>\n        </h1>\n        <p>\n         Web components that extend Bootstrap 4.\n        </p>\n       </div>\n       <h2>\n        Installation\n       </h2>\n       <div class="row">\n        <div class="col-xs-12 col-sm-6">\n         <h3>\n          Compiled\n         </h3>\n         <p>\n          Minified CSS and JavaScript with no  documentation or original source files.\n         </p>\n         <code>\n          bower install vuestrap-base-components --save-dev\n         </code>\n        </div>\n        <div class="col-xs-12 col-sm-6">\n         <h3>\n          Source\n         </h3>\n         <p>\n          Source Sass, JavaScript, and documentation files.\n         </p>\n         <code>\n          npm install vuestrap-base-components --save-dev\n         </code>\n        </div>\n       </div>\n       <div class="m-b-lg">\n       </div>\n       <h2>\n        Usage\n       </h2>\n       <p>\n        For compiled components, use it within your Vue instance like this:\n       </p>\n       <p>\n        <code>\n         new Vue({ components: { \'vs-alert\': vuestrapBase.alert }})\n        </code>\n       </p>\n       <div class="m-b">\n       </div>\n       <strong>\n        OR\n       </strong>\n       <div class="m-b">\n       </div>\n       <p>\n        If you chosen to work with source components, just import* desired component like so:\n       </p>\n       <p>\n        <code>\n         import { vsAlert } from \'vuestrap-base-components/src/components\'\n        </code>\n       </p>\n       <p>\n        and then load it in your Vue instance:\n       </p>\n       <p>\n        <code>\n         new Vue({ components: { vsAlert }})\n        </code>\n       </p>\n       <p>\n        *Note: You will need\n        <a href="https://github.com/babel/babel-loader">\n         Babel Loader\n        </a>\n        in your Webpack config file to support ES6 syntax.\n       </p>\n       <div class="m-b-lg">\n       </div>\n       <h2>\n        Examples\n       </h2>\n       <ul>\n        <li>\n         <a href="examples/basic.html" target="_blank">\n          Basic example of a landing page with selected components.\n         </a>\n        </li>\n        <li>\n         <a href="http://kzima.github.io/vuestrap-starter/" target="_blank">\n          Advanced example\n         </a>\n         with webpack config and theme implementation - (\n         <a href="https://github.com/kzima/vuestrap-starter" target="_blank">\n          source on github\n         </a>\n         )\n        </li>\n       </ul>\n       <div class="m-b-lg">\n       </div>\n       <h2>\n        Theming\n       </h2>\n       <p>\n        To be able to use your app theme with component\'s scss variables, you will need to use\n        <a href="https://github.com/kzima/vueastrap-theme-loader">\n         vuestrap-theme-loader\n        </a>\n        in your webpack config file.\n       </p>\n       <p>\n        <code>\n         npm install vuestrap-theme-loader --save-dev\n        </code>\n       </p>\n       <p>\n        See\n        <a href="https://github.com/kzima/vuestrap-starter">\n         vuestrap-starter\n        </a>\n        for a webpack config example with theme loader.\n       </p>\n      </div>\n      <!-- /col-xs-12 -->\n      <!-- sidebar -->\n      <div class="col-xs-12 col-md-3 sidebar-offcanvas
